        function fmtDate(oTime){
            var cTime = new Date().getTime()
            if (oTime == null) {
                return "";
            }
            else {
                var millisecond = cTime - oTime;
                var minute = 60 * 1000;
                var hour = minute * 60;
                var day = hour * 24;

                if (millisecond <= minute) {
                    return "刚刚";
                } else if (millisecond > minute && millisecond <= hour) {
                    var  minuteNum = millisecond / minute;
                    return Math.round(minuteNum) + " 分钟前";
                } else if (millisecond > hour && millisecond <= day) {
                    var hourNum = millisecond / hour;
                    return Math.round(hourNum) + " 小时前";
                } else {
                    da = new Date(oTime);
                    var year = da.getFullYear()+'-';
                    var month = da.getMonth()+1+'-';
                    var day = da.getDate();
                    return year+month+day
                }
            }
        }

        var myScroll;
        var pullDownEl, pullDownL;
        var pullUpEl, pullUpL;
        var loadingStep = 0; //加载状态0默认，1显示加载状态，2执行加载数据，只有当为0时才能再次加载，这是防止过快拉动刷新
        var reciepid = 1580;
        var Upcount = 1;
        var lastpage = 0;
        var pagedata;
        function requestData(pageno, perpage, recipeid) //获取服务器数据
        {
            $.ajax({
                type: "get",
                url: "/v1/recipecomment/more?pageno=" + pageno + "&perpage=" + perpage + "&recipeid=" + recipeid,
                cache: true,
                async: false, //异步会有刷新不到数据的情况
                success: function (result) {
                    pagedata = "";
                    if(result.result.length<=0)
					{
                        if(pageno<=1)
                        {
                            var nolist = "<li>"+
                                    "<div class='conter'>"+
                                    "<div style='min-height: 50px;padding: 15px 10px 0px 0px;position: relative;padding-bottom: 5px;'>"+
                                    "<div class='f-user-info' style='margin: 0px;padding: 0px;'>"+
                                    "<div class='f-nick' style='width: 100%;white-space: nowrap;word-wrap: normal;overflow: hidden;text-overflow: ellipsis;font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;margin-bottom: 8px;'><a href='#' style='     display: block;float: left;width: 100px;color: #f57f0c;text-decoration: none;'>"+"</a>"+
                                    "<span href='#' style='color: #8C8C8C;font-size: 12px;float: right;margin-right: 10px;'>"+"</span>"+
                                    "</div>"+
                                    "<div class='info-detail' style='margin: 0px;padding: 0px; text-align: center'><span class=' ui-mr8 state' style='display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;color: #8C8C8C;line-height: 1.334;font-size: 15px;    padding-bottom: 8px;'>"+"暂无相关评论，去发表个评论吧"+"</span></div>"+
                                    "</div>"+
                                    "</div>"+
                                    "</div>"+
                                    "</li>";
                            $('#add').append(nolist);
                        }
                        loadingStep = -1;
                        lastpage = -1;
					}else
					{
                        $.each(result.result, function (index, item) {
                            var owninfo = "";
                            var ownpic= "/core/api/img/my.png";
                            if(item.userName != null)
                            {
                                owninfo = item.userName;
                            }else
                            {
                                owninfo = "压力锅用户";
                            }
                            if(item.headPic != null)
                            {
                                ownpic=item.headPic;
                            }
                            pagedata += "<li>"+
                                    "<div class='conter'>"+
                                    "<div style='min-height: 50px;padding: 15px 10px 0px 60px;position: relative;padding-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid #ccc;'>"+
                                    "<div class='f-user-pto' style='position: absolute;left: 9px;top: 15px;'>"+
                                    "<a href='' style='background: url("+ownpic+") no-repeat;position: relative;background-size: 100% 100%;display: block;border: 0px none;font-size: 0px;width: 40px;height: 40px;vertical-align: top;border-radius: 4px;'></a>"+
                                    "</div>"+
                                    "<div class='f-user-info' style='margin: 0px;padding: 0px;'>"+
                                    "<div class='f-nick' style='width: 100%;white-space: nowrap;word-wrap: normal;overflow: hidden;text-overflow: ellipsis;font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;margin-bottom: 8px;'><a href='#' style='     display: block;float: left;width: 100px;color: #f57f0c;text-decoration: none;'>"+owninfo+"</a>"+
                                    "<span href='#' style='color: #8C8C8C;font-size: 12px;float: right;margin-right: 10px;'>"+fmtDate(item.commentTime)+"</span>"+
                                    "</div>"+
                                    "<div class='info-detail' style='margin: 0px;padding: 0px;'><span class=' ui-mr8 state' style='display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;color: #8C8C8C;line-height: 1.334;font-size: 12px;    padding-bottom: 8px;'>"+item.contents+"</span></div>"+
                                    "</div>"+
                                    "</div>"+
                                    "</div>"+
                                    "</li>";
                        });
					}

                    Upcount++;
                }
            });
        }
        function pullUpAction() { //上拉事件
            var el, li, i;
            el = $('#add');
            requestData(Upcount, 18, reciepid);
            el.append(pagedata);
            pullUpEl.removeClass('loading');
            pullUpL.html('上拉显示更多...');
            pullUpEl['class'] = pullUpEl.attr('class');
            pullUpEl.attr('class', '').hide();
            myScroll.refresh();
            loadingStep = 0;
        }

        function loaded() {
            pullDownEl = $('#pullDown');
            pullDownL = pullDownEl.find('.pullDownLabel');
            pullDownEl['class'] = pullDownEl.attr('class');
            pullDownEl.attr('class', '').hide();
            pullUpEl = $('#pullUp');
            pullUpL = pullUpEl.find('.pullUpLabel');
            pullUpEl['class'] = pullUpEl.attr('class');
            pullUpEl.attr('class', '').hide();
            myScroll = new IScroll('#content', {
                probeType: 2, //probeType：1对性能没有影响。在滚动事件被触发时，滚动轴是不是忙着做它的东西。probeType：2总执行滚动，除了势头，反弹过程中的事件。这类似于原生的onscroll事件。probeType：3发出的滚动事件与到的像素精度。注意，滚动被迫requestAnimationFrame（即：useTransition：假）。
                scrollbars: true, //有滚动条
                mouseWheel: true, //允许滑轮滚动
                fadeScrollbars: true, //滚动时显示滚动条，默认影藏，并且是淡出淡入效果
                bounce: true, //边界反弹
                interactiveScrollbars: true, //滚动条可以拖动
                shrinkScrollbars: 'scale', // 当滚动边界之外的滚动条是由少量的收缩。'clip' or 'scale'.
                click: true, // 允许点击事件
                keyBindings: true, //允许使用按键控制
                momentum: true // 允许有惯性滑动
            });
            //滚动时
            myScroll.on('scroll', function() {
                        if (loadingStep == 0 && !pullDownEl.attr('class').match('flip|loading') && !pullUpEl.attr('class').match('flip|loading')) {
                            if (this.y < (this.maxScrollY + 400)) {
                                if (this.maxScrollY != 0 && this.y < (this.maxScrollY + 400)) {
                                    // 上拉刷新效果
                                    pullUpEl.attr('class', pullUpEl['class'])
                                    pullUpEl.show();
                                    myScroll.refresh();
                                    pullUpEl.addClass('flip');
                                    pullUpL.html("拼命加载中...");
                                    loadingStep = 1;
                                }
                                if (lastpage == -1) {
                                    loadingStep = -1;
                                }
                            }
                        } else {
                            if (lastpage == -1) {
                                pullUpEl.show();
                                pullUpL.html("已经是最后一页");
                                loadingStep = -1;
                            }
                        }
                    }

            );
            //滚动完毕
            myScroll.on('scrollEnd', function() {
                if (loadingStep == 1) {
                    if (pullUpEl.attr('class').match('flip|loading')) {
                        pullUpEl.removeClass('flip').addClass('loading');
                        pullUpL.html('Loading...');
                        loadingStep = 2;
                        pullUpAction();
                    }
                }else if (loadingStep == -1){
                pullUpEl.removeClass('loading');
                pullUpEl['class'] = pullUpEl.attr('class');
                pullUpEl.attr('class', '').hide();
                myScroll.refresh();
                loadingStep = 0;
            }
            });
        }
        document.addEventListener('touchmove', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
        }, false);

        function initlist() { //first init
            requestData(Upcount, 18, reciepid);
            $("#add").append(pagedata);
            loaded();
        }
        $(document).ready(function() {
            initlist(); //初始化iscokll
        });

    </script>
